# Update Playlist app model based on an action #

let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList = 
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
    | AddSong(song) =>
      let songs, current = playlist in
      if (current == NoSongSelected) then
        let new_playlist = (song::songs, PausedOn(song) ) in 
          new_playlist
      else

# Update Playlist app model based on an action #

let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList = 
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
    | AddSong(song) =>
      let songs, current = playlist in
      if (current == NoSongSelected) then
        let new_playlist = (song::songs, PausedOn(song) ) in 
          new_playlist
      else 
        let new_playlist = (song::songs, current ) in

# Update Playlist app model based on an action #

let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList = 
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
    | AddSong(song) =>
      let songs, current = playlist in
      if (current == NoSongSelected) then
        let new_playlist = (song::songs, PausedOn(song) ) in 
          new_playlist
      else 
        let new_playlist = (song::songs, current ) in
        new_playlist

# Update Playlist app model based on an action #

let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList = 
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
    | AddSong(song) =>
      let songs, current = playlist in
      if (current == NoSongSelected) then
        let new_playlist = (song::songs, PausedOn(song) ) in 
          new_playlist
      else 
        let new_playlist = (song::songs, current ) in
        new_playlist
      end

# Update Playlist app model based on an action #

let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList = 
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
    | AddSong(song) =>
      let songs, current = playlist in
      if (current == NoSongSelected) then
        let new_playlist = (song::songs, PausedOn(song) ) in 
          new_playlist
      else 
        let new_playlist = (song::songs, current ) in
        new_playlist
      end

# Update Playlist app model based on an action #

let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList = 
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
    | AddSong(song) =>
      let songs, current = playlist in
      if (current == NoSongSelected) then
        let new_playlist = (song::songs, PausedOn(song) ) in 
          new_playlist
      else 
        let new_playlist = (song::songs, current ) in
        new_playlist
      end
